 3 Strength

@856    = ~The journal lists a number of experiments, apparently conducted by a mage known as Lium the Lucky. The section dealing with the machine in front of you draws your eye:

"What a wondrous contraption! It creates, enchants, and dispenses magical equipment of no small power by pulling these six levers in the correct order. The ranking of the levers seems to change daily, and pulling them in the incorrect order results in painful and instant death, as I've deduced from the bloodstains on the floor. I've gotten the order correct for the last few days and sent the items home with Pooky. It is well that I found the machine when I did, for it hasn't much life left. Each item it creates damages the inner workings further, and soon I fear it shall fall apart. The previous order was:
1) Ruby
2) Jade
3) Mithral
4) Onyx
5) Emerald
6) Sandalwood.

I've taken apart what pieces of the machine I could, and found the device that sets the ranking of the levers. With it, as stated, the order for the past several days was clear. Now the cursed thing has broken and I've garnered hardly any information from it at all. This is what I *have* discovered:
A) The jade lever's change in ranking was the greatest of the six levers.
B) The product of the onyx lever's rankings for the two days (when multiplied) is same as the product of the sandalwood lever's last two rankings when multiplied.
C) None of the levers are ever in the exact same place in line as they were yesterday.
D) Obviously, due to the change in the jade lever's order, there are only two possibilities regarding the change in the orders of the onyx and sandalwood levers, one of which contradicts another clue.
E) It is likely that the mithral lever moved the same number of rankings as the sandalwood lever.

Quite the dilemma and the guesswork is risky. However, the items I've obtained are worth the risk and, with logic, I'm sure that I'll discover the correct order for today."

The journal says no more.《這本日誌中列出幾種實驗，顯然是一個叫做「幸運李溫」的法師所寫的。關於你眼前這些機器的部分吸引了你的注意力：

「好奇妙的設計！只要依照正確的順序來拉動這六道拉桿，就可以創造、施法及除去威力強大的魔法裝備。拉桿的排列好像每天都會改變，而且若是以不正確的順序來拉動它們，就會導致痛苦和立時的死亡－－這是我從地上的血跡研判出來的。我已經找出最後幾天的正確順序，並且叫波奇把東西送回家。還好，當我找到這部機器時，它已經沒有剩下多少能量了。每當它造成傷害時，它的內裡就會動得更厲害，我怕它會瓦解。先前的順序是：
1）	紅寶石
2）	玉
3）	秘銀
4）	縞瑪瑙
5）	綠寶石
6）	檀香

我盡量把機器拆開來，發現設定拉桿順序的裝置。因此我找出過去幾天的順序。現在那個該死的東西已經壞了，我幾乎無法再收集到什麼資料。到目前為止，我的發現如下：
A）	玉拉桿的順序變動是六根拉桿中最大的。
B）	縞瑪瑙兩天順序的乘積（順序相乘之後）就和檀木後兩次順序的乘積相同。
C）	所有拉桿的位置都不會和前一天相同。
D）	很顯然地，由於玉拉桿的順序改變，因此縞瑪瑙和檀香拉桿的順序變化只有兩種可能性，二者正好相反。
E）	看起來秘銀拉桿移動的數目和檀香拉桿的順序相同。

這種猜測相當冒險。但是，我拿到的東西值得冒這個險，而且，透過邏輯，我相信我已經找到今天的正確順序了。」

日誌沒有別的記錄了。》~

@2575   = ~Spacewarp
(Alteration)

Sphere: Numbers
Range: 150 ft.
Duration: 1 turn
Casting Time: 7
Area of Effect: 25-ft. radius sphere
Saving Throw: None

According to one view of the universe, what we perceive as gravity is actually a localized warping of the fabric of space-time. The Spacewarp spell creates a temporary but very intense warping in a limited area.

When the priest casts this spell, <PRO_HESHE> selects a specific point to be the center of effect. This point may be anywhere within 150 feet of the caster, including in midair.

When the spell is completed, this center of effect gains a gravity field equal to the force felt at the surface of the earth. In other words, gravity is centered at this point; everything within 50 feet of this center that is not attached to something immovable will fall toward the selected point.

This localized gravity affects only loose objects and creatures capable of movement (i.e., not trees, whose roots are buried in the ground). It does not affect the ground itself—soil, plants, desert sand, lake water, etc. are immune to the effect.《空間變換（改變系）
領域：數字
有效距離：50碼
持續時間：10輪
施法時間：7
影響範圍：直徑50尺方圓
豁免檢定：無

根據某種宇宙論，我們所感受到的重力實際上是一種以特定區域為中心的時空扭曲現象。空間變換法術能夠在有限的區域當中，創造出一道短暫，但是卻非常強烈的時空扭曲。
當牧師施展這法術時，他必須選擇一個特定的點作為法術作用的中心區域。這個點可以是距離施法者50碼範圍內的任何一點，包括半空中。
當法術完成後，法術效用的中心會產生幾乎等同於站在地表上所感覺到的重力場。也就是說，重力會以選定的作為點為中心；任何距離中心點50尺範圍內的東西，如果沒有和不可移動的物品連結在一起，都會跌向施術者所選定的作用中心。
這道局部的重力只會影響到鬆散的物品，或者具有移動能力的生物（例如，樹木便不會受影響，它們的根紮在地上固定著）。這法術並不會影響到地面上原有的物品－－泥土、植物、沙漠裡的沙子、湖裡的水等等，皆不會受此法術影響。》~

Every Corthala who has used their magical talents has become obsessed with them and ultimately come to a grievous end. Valygar intends to fulfill his family's oath to find and destroy their ancestor, Lavok, and then he intends to let his cursed bloodline die out once and for all. 《當被問起他的過去時，瓦裡格沉默了好一陣子，臉色變得相當凝重。他簡短地解釋道，寇薩拉家族曾經是安姆最富裕的貴族，但如今卻僅存他孤身一人。寇薩拉家族一直都被魔法的能力所詛咒，然而，瓦裡格卻是帶著極大的諷刺意味說出這幾些話。每個使用他們魔法天賦的寇薩拉家人，都會為魔法的力量所著迷，最後也都落入極為悲慘的下場。他的母親就是近來最好的例證，但是瓦裡格對此並沒有說得十分清楚。瓦裡格打算要完成他們家族的誓言，找到並且摧毀他們的祖先拉沃克，然後他計劃就這麼讓自己身上飽受詛咒的血脈就此劃下句點。》~

@2968   = ~Magic Missile《魔法飛彈》~
@2969   = ~Invisibility 
(Illusion/Phantasm)

Level: 2
Range: Touch 
Duration: Special 
Casting Time: 2 
Area of Effect: 1 creature 
Saving Throw: None 

This spell causes the creature touched to vanish from sight and be undetectable by normal vision or even infravision. Of course, the invisible creature is not magically silenced, and certain other conditions can render the creature detectable. Even allies cannot see the invisible creature or its gear, unless these allies can normally see invisible things or employ magic to do so. Items dropped or put down by the invisible creature become visible; items picked up disappear if tucked into the clothing or pouches worn by the creature. The spell remains in effect until it is magically broken or dispelled, until the recipient attacks any creature, or until 24 hours have passed. The caster cannot perform any actions that manipulate the environment around <PRO_HIMHER>, such as opening doors, disarming a trap, or opening a chest. The caster can, however, cast defensive spells on <PRO_HIMHER>self and fellow party members. And if <PRO_HESHE> attacks, <PRO_HESHE> immediately becomes visible, although the invisibility enables <PRO_HIMHER> to attack first.《隱形術
（幻術/魅影系）

等級：2
有效距離：碰觸
持續時間：特殊
施法時間：2
影響範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：無

這個法術可使其他人看不見被碰觸到的生物，連夜視能力也無法加以偵測。當然，如果這個隱形生物發出聲音，或是遇到其他特殊狀況，他還是會被發現。即使盟友也無法看見這個隱形生物以及他的裝備，除非他本來就可以看見隱形生物或是可以施展破除隱形的魔法。隱形生物放下的物品會恢復為可見狀態，而他們若將物品撿起塞到背包或是衣服裡面，該物品也會變成隱形。這個法術失效的狀況如下：被其他魔法解除、受術者攻擊任何生物，或者是經過二十四小時的時間。此外，該隱形生物也不可以進行會影響到週遭環境的直接動作，例如開門、解除陷阱，或是打開箱子。但是他卻可以施展防禦性法術在自己或者隊友身上。如果他進行任何攻擊行為，隱形效果就會立即失效，不過隱形狀態卻能讓他擁有先攻優勢。》~

STATISTICS:

Weight: 2《吸血鬼的形成

這本書被泡在血裡，破壞了裡面大部分的書頁。原來的墨汁已經完全不可辨識。書緣上最近寫下的筆跡留下一種印象，四處留下幾個字，剛好可以說明這本書的內容。這本書顯然說明了成為吸血鬼的程序，不過你看不出來為什麼會有人想要這麼做。書背上有一個印痕，顯示這本曾經為歐瑪的跟隨者所保有及記錄。

@4193   = ~This text is written in a very old dialect of southern Common that you are not familiar with, though it does not appear to be a particularly ancient tome. It seems to be a section of the personal journal of a noble named Tomass Sangui and deals with the acquiring and control of his most devoted servants. It is difficult to ascertain much more, though from the frequency of certain words, you are reasonably sure that Tomass was creating vampire minions, if not some other creature that feeds on blood. His knowledge on the subject seems quite intimate indeed, and he details the long process of completely turning a victim. Apparently, if the process is interrupted, it can be reversed, but the author does not say how. There is a stamp on the back of the book that indicates it was once archived and recorded by the followers of Oghma.

STATISTICS:

Weight: 2《召喚歐塔僕人法

這本書用一種南方非常古老的方言寫成，你並不熟悉，不過這看起來並不是什麼古老的書冊。看起來它似乎是個叫做托瑪斯·桑貴的貴族的私人日誌，內容是關於購買及控制他最忠心的僕人。很難再進一步肯定什麼，不過從某些字出現的頻率來看，你可以確定托瑪斯正在製造吸血鬼手下，不然就是別的以血為食的怪物。他對於這個主題的瞭解似乎相當深入，而且他詳細記載將獵物徹底轉變的過程。很顯然地，如果這個過程被打斷，仍然可以回轉，但是作者並沒有說明如何做。書背上有一個印痕，顯示這本曾經為歐瑪的跟隨者所保有及記錄。

@4396   = ~This journal was found on the body of the shadow-slain warrior that you stumbled upon near the entrance to the dark woods. The last entry is of particular interest:

"Nothing is as I'd imagined that it would be. I expected to become a hero when I joined Mazzy Fentan's party. I expected that we would slay monsters with ease and bask in the glory of victory as they do in the old tales. But it is not as it seems.

I did not expect the drudgery of the march, the casual horror of slaughter, the smell of death everywhere. I swear I can taste it! We've killed so many shadows and black wolves that my brain has become as numb as my arm. I am covered in ichor but have not the energy to even clean myself.

If not for Mazzy, I think that I would be mad. She is a constant source of strength and always reminds us of the innocents that these beasts have killed, of the horror that we must take upon ourselves to save the people who have no defense. Mazzy is the hero here, not I.

The battle has only just begun. Today we arrived at the entrance to the ruined temple. It was crawling with shadows. Were it not for Mazzy's quick thinking, we would surely be dead. There were far too many to fight, but Mazzy used the stained glass of the ruins to reflect what light we had, illuminating the entrance and sending the shades to their doom. While the stained glass caught the light, we were able to find a pocket of safety. Any shadows that came within were destroyed by the light.

Tomorrow we will attempt to enter the temple and the darkness. I have never felt such dread. I try to be as brave as Mazzy but cannot. I feel the horrible, inescapable urge to run, and when the battle is joined, I can only hope that I will not."

STATISTICS:

Weight: 2《這本日誌是在你靠近黑暗森林入口附近遇到的那個被鬼魂殺死的戰士屍體上找到的。最後一筆記錄尤其有趣：

「所有事情都和我想像的不一樣。當我加入瑪茲·芬頓的隊伍時，我期盼能成為英雄。我以為我們可以輕易殺死怪物，沐浴在勝利的光榮之中，就像古老的故事中所描述的一樣。但是並不是這個樣子。

我沒有料想到行進的辛苦，殺戮的恐怖，到處都是的死亡氣息。我發誓我可以嘗到它！我們殺了這麼多的鬼魂和黑狼，我的頭腦變得和我的手臂一樣遲鈍。我會身都是膿水，但是沒有力氣去清理。

若不是瑪茲的話，我想我會瘋了。她是力量的來源，而且總是提醒我們想起這些野獸殺死的無辜者，還有我們要肩負的恐怖，以拯救那些沒有能力自保的人。瑪茲才是英雄，不是我。

戰鬥才剛開始。今天我們到達廢棄神殿的入口。裡面都是鬼魂。若不是瑪茲腦筋動得快，我們一定已經死了。鬼魂的數量太多，但是瑪茲利用廢墟的彩色玻璃反射我們所擁有的光線，照亮入口，毀掉那些鬼魂。當彩色玻璃反射光線時，我們得以找到一個安全的地方。任何走到範圍內的鬼魂都被光線所殺。

明天我們會試著進入神殿及黑暗之中。我從來不曾感到這麼害怕。我試著和瑪茲一樣勇敢，但是我做不到。我感受到無法抗拒的想要逃走的衝動，當戰鬥開始時，我只希望我不會逃走。」

@4736   = ~Improved Invisibility
(Illusion/Phantasm)

Level: 4
Range: Touch
Duration: 3 rounds + 1 round/level
Casting Time: 4
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: None

This spell is similar to Invisibility, but the recipient is able to attack by missile discharge, melee combat, or spellcasting while remaining unseen. However, telltale traces—a shimmering—allow an observant opponent to attack the invisible spell recipient. These traces are only noticeable when specifically looked for (after the invisible character has made <PRO_HISHER> presence known). Attacks against the invisible character suffer a -4 penalty to attack rolls, and the invisible character's Saving Throws are made with a +4 bonus.

Note: After making an attack, the wizard is no longer completely invisible. Opponents can target the wizard.《高等隱形術
（幻術/魅影系）

等級：4
有效距離：觸碰
持續時間：3輪+1輪/每等級
施法時間：4
影響範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：無

這個法術和隱形術類似，但是受術者可以進行攻擊，不管是使用遠程武器、近身肉搏或是施法都可以繼續保持隱形。不過，細微的痕跡——即使是微光——都可能使敵人攻擊隱形者。這樣的跡象只有特別加以注意才會發現（當隱形的人物讓大家知道<PRO_HISHER>存在之後）。攻擊隱形的人物時在命中檢定上會有-4的不利修正，而隱形者的豁免檢定則擁有+4的獎勵。

注意：進行攻擊行為之後，受術者將不再保持完全隱形的狀態，能夠成為被敵人攻擊的目標。》~

@6065   = ~Poison
(Necromancy)

Level: 4
Range: 15 ft.
Duration: 1 turn
Casting Time: 4
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: Neg.

Through this spell, the caster can poison victims who fail their Saving Throw vs. Poison. The damage inflicted depends on the level of the caster as detailed below:
 7–9th level: 2d8 + 2/round
 10–12th level: 3d8 + 3/round
 13–14th level: 4d8 + 4/round
 15–16th level: 6d8 + 5/round
 17+ level: 8d8 + 6/round
Those who make their Saving Throws are unaffected.《毒素
（死靈系）

等級：4
有效距離：15呎
持續時間：1回合
施法時間：4
影響範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：通過則無效

施展此法術可以讓施法者對目標下毒，若目標未能通過對毒素的豁免檢定則會中毒。法術傷害施法者的等級決定：
	7-9級：2d8+2/輪
	10-12級：3d8+3/輪
	13-14級：4d8+4/輪
	15-16級：6d8+5/輪
	17級以上：8d8+6/輪

目標如通過對毒素的豁免檢定將不會受到後續中毒效果的影響。》~

@6088   = ~Holy Power
(Evocation)

Level: 4
Range: 0
Duration: 1 round/level
Casting Time: 6
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None

Through this spell, the caster imbues <PRO_HIMHER>self with the strength and skill of a Fighter of the same level. The priest's Strength score is set to 18/00—even if it is normally higher—<PRO_HISHER> THAC0 becomes that of a Fighter of the same level, and <PRO_HESHE> gains 1 temporary Hit Point per level. This will last for the duration of the spell or until dispelled.《神聖之力
（塑能系）

等級：4
領域：戰鬥
有效距離：無
持續時間：1輪/每等級
施法時間：6
影響範圍：施法者
豁免檢定：無

此法術可以使施法者擁有相同等級之戰士般的力量和技能。牧師的力量將設為18/00——即使原來比較高也一樣——<PRO_HISHER>零級命中值變成等於相同等級的戰士，並且 <PRO_HESHE>可獲得每級1點臨時生命值。這個法術會一直持續到有效時間結束，或是被解除魔法為止。》~
